**13:03** `Deleted Account`: psychological

. If people then start to raise their pitch or speak louder, this is a sign that they are defending themselves as they speak. By contrast, liars would want to hide their nervousness and unconscious feelings of guilt with a conspicuously quiet pitch. If someone speaks abnormally quickly or slowly, this is also an indication of dishonesty. Again, as soon as something seems strange to you and doesn't feel good, it could be that you are being fooled.
